## 1. 一句话总览

V1.5 已完工并打 milestone；V2 (AI-native office) 在两个会话内完成了
**W2 S4 controller** 落地、**W3 utf8 边界 fixture**、**W5 schema +
fixtures + 终态 fixture + reader's manual** 全套 documentation-tier
+ harness、**W4 schema + fixtures + H5 partial-enforce** 全套。
当前阻塞点：**W2 D3.3b Cmd+K 冲突**（B1，A/B 待拍）、**W3 Day-1b** /
**W4 Day-0** / **W5 Day-0 C++** 等授权（D1/Scope）、**B2** 本地无法
编译、**F2** 推送被禁。**5 个 V2 contract harness 全绿**（按 L62 之前
口径；post-L62 升至 7 个 H1-H7，自 §13 之后用 7 口径，本段保留时间戳
原文）。

## 2. 仓库形态

```
BUILDDIR  /Users/lu/可点office          # 配置过的 LibreOffice 风格构建树
SRCDIR    /Users/lu/kdoffice-src        # 源码 git checkout
INSTDIR   instdir/可圈office.app        # macOS app bundle 输出位
WORKDIR   workdir/                      # gbuild 中间产物
```

- BUILDDIR 顶层 `Makefile` 是 autogen 生成的，模块快捷键如
  `make sw.build` / `make sc.build` 走 `solenv/gbuild/partial_build.mk`。
- `instdir/` 现状: `Contents/` 存在但近乎空 → 没有可运行的 .app。
- `workdir/` 有目录结构 (CppunitTest/CxxObject/...) 但是 fresh state，
  非全量构建产物。

## 5. 路线图与各 Wave 状态

### V1.5 ✅ 已完工 (milestone `2026-05-08-v1.5-completion`)

- zh-CN i18n 全套 / 商务模板 + 可圈office 品牌资产 / macOS web/template
  iconset 刷新 / workbench UITest smoke 套件 / IconHelper / tray /
  sidebar 视觉精修 / 27/27 strict roundtrip baseline 锁定。

### V2 (`2026-05-08-v2-ai-native`) — AI-native office

| Wave | 焦点 | 状态 |
|---|---|---|
| W1 | Provider runtime (Ollama-first 沙箱) | 主体已落地 + 51 cppunit |
| W2 | Cmd+K 命令调色板 | Controller cppunit 落地（S4）；**D3.3b 卡 Cmd+K 冲突等 B1 拍板** |
| W3 | Writer apply-runtime + ApplyPlan validator | Day-1{a,c-h} ✅, **Day-1b ⛔ 待 D1**; utf8 multi-codepoint fixture L44 |
| W4 | Select-to-act 浮窗 / Diff 审批 | spec + Day-0 plan + enum lock (L37) + **schema + 4 fixtures + H5 partial-enforce (L46)** |
| W5 | Async cowork (长任务 + diff review) | spec + Day-0 plan + token lock (L37) + **schema + fixtures + 终态 fixture + reader's manual + H4 partial-enforce (L41+L43+L45)** |

**ai-native cppunit 总数**: **84** cases
（51 provider + 33 cui = 8 idx + 8 fuzzy + 10 recent + 7 controller）。

| Day-1h | ✅ | `tests/v2-provider-evidence-schema-test.sh` schema↔C++ drift lock |

### W4 — 详情 (schema + H5 L46)

Spec + Day-0 Entry-Point Plan + **Action enum lock** (L37) +
**schema + 4 fixtures + H5 partial-enforce** (L46)。

`docs/schemas/inline-action-request.schema.json`:
- 7 top-level required keys + `additionalProperties:false` + 3-branch
  `oneOf` keyed on `surface` const
- writer-paragraph 分支锁 ParagraphAction 7 token
- calc-cell 分支锁 CellAction 5 token
- impress-slide-element 分支锁 SlideElementAction 4 token

4 个 fixture: `valid` (writer rewrite minimal) / `calc-suggest-chart`
(extended-naming) / `impress-translate` (extended-naming) /
`invalid` (9 violations)。

H5 (`tests/v2-inline-action-request-schema-test.sh`) partial-enforce
模式 — schema oneOf 3 branch 锁 + 每分支 action enum 顺序锁 + 4
fixture 验证；当
`${KDOFFICE_SRC_ROOT}/sw|sc|sd/source/.../inline-actions/*.hxx` 全部
落地时自动升级到 full-enforce。

C++ 仍 gated（`sw/source/uibase/inline-actions/` /
`sc/source/ui/inline-actions/` / `sd/source/ui/inline-actions/` /
`svx/source/sidebar/diff-review/`）。

### W5 — 详情 (full doc-tier landed L41+L43+L45)

Spec + Day-0 Entry-Point Plan + **Token lock** (L37) + **schema**
(L41) + **valid + invalid + terminal-failed fixtures** (L41+L43) +
**reader's manual** (`async-task.schema.md` L45) +
**H4 partial-enforce** 模式。

3 个 fixture 覆盖矩阵:
- `async-task.valid.json` — awaiting-review happy path
- `async-task.invalid.json` — 11 distinct violations
- `async-task.terminal-failed.json` — `state=failed` + `failure_reason`
  + `result_plan_id=null` 边界

C++ 仍 gated（`kqoffice/source/ai/cowork/**` +
`kqoffice/qa/cppunit/test_cowork*`）。

## 6. 当前阻塞 (ordered by 紧急度)

### 🔴 B1 — Cmd+K 快捷键冲突

`Accelerators.xcu:93` `K_MOD1` 已绑定 `.uno:HyperlinkDialog`。

**待用户拍板 A/B**:
- **A**: 抢占 K_MOD1 → CommandPalette。代价: HyperlinkDialog 失去 Cmd+K（Word/Pages/Google Docs 全行业 Cmd+K=Hyperlink）。
- **B** (推荐): CommandPalette → MOD1_SHIFT+K (Cmd+Shift+K)。代价: 偏离 spec，但零回归。

### 🟡 B2 — 无法本地编译验证

`sfx2.build` 失败 (`concat-deps: No such file or directory` +
`gb_Deliver_deliver: ... libsal_textenclo.dylib ...`)。
依赖未来有 build infra 的 session 补 verify。

### 🟢 B3 — 远端推送被禁

F2 决策: 无 SSH key + HTTPS 2GB pack 触 500MB 限制。
SRCDIR ahead origin **18** commits，全部本地。

## 13. 晚间增量 (2026-05-11 evening, L47→L78)

> 本节为 morning snapshot (L46 close-out) 的 append-only 续写。第
> 1–12 节是 L46 时点冻结视图，下面是同日 evening 截至 L78 的增量；
> 如果两节冲突，**evening 节为准**（生成时间更晚）。

### 13.1 一句话变化

5 harness → **7 harness**（H6 reader's-manual coherence + H7 apply-plan-runtime），
H2 baseline 26 checks → **45**（新增 7-15 共 9 个 lock）；ledger 46 → **78 行**；
fixtures 34 → **36/13**；OK(84) cppunit claimed 不变但**workdir verify 77** +
B2 阻塞 upgrade-path（L75 honest split）。无新 wave landed，
全是 documentation/locking/honesty-correction tier 工作面。

### 13.2 新增 harness (相对 §6)

| Harness | Lock | 落定 |
|---|---|---|
| H6 `v2-schema-manual-coherence-test.sh` | 4 reader's manual fact-block ↔ schema body bidirectional | L58/L59（glob-discovered + 5-key allow-list）|
| H7 `v2-apply-plan-runtime-schema-test.sh` | W3 schema kind enum order ↔ spec table + envelope guards (**partial**) | L55 |

`bin/v2-harness-sweep.sh` (L65) 是 7-harness 单次入口；`--with-fixtures`
追加 V1.5+V2 fixture 跑 + ≥36/0 断言。CI workflow paths-filter (L73)
覆盖 sweep 脚本 + ledger 目录。

### 13.3 H2 新增 check (7→15, 相对 §6)

| # | Lock | 落定 | Drift class |
|---|---|---|---|
| 7 | W4 + W5 specs Day-0 Entry-Point Plan 段 | pre-L62 | Day-0 spec 完整性 |
| 8 | W4 + W5 specs enum-lock 子节 | pre-L62 | enum 漂移 |
| 9 | lane-status.md `(N entries)` = `wc -l` ledger | pre-L62 | ledger 计数撒谎 |
| 10 | reader's manual ↔ lane-status bidirectional | L58 | 文件存在但未引 / 引用但无文件 |
| 11 | lane-status 引 `tests/v2-*.sh` 路径存在 + 0755 | L60 | 重命名/掉权限 |
| 12 | ledger 行 canonical 4-key shape | L66 | L65 事件：drop `event` key |
| 13 | pass-count baseline 3-site 镜像 (CLAUDE-NOTES + handoff + sweep header) | L67 | 单点 bump 漏其他 |
| 14 | `bin/v2-harness-sweep.sh` exec-bit | L70 | sweep silently fails permission |
| 15 | sweep enumeration ↔ disk parity (双向) | L76 | 新 harness 不进 sweep / sweep 引不存在的 |

每个 check 12-15 都有 inline negative-canary（CLAUDE-NOTES
§"Verifying check 12/13/14/15 actually catch drift"，L69 起 +
L77 扩展），touch 时跑过证明 lock 真抓 drift class。

### 13.4 4-tier locking architecture (post-L67/L76)

1. Schema body ↔ C++ tokens (H1 full / H4/H5/H7 partial)
2. Schema body ↔ reader's manual fact-block (H6, glob-discovered)
3. lane-status ↔ on-disk artifacts (H2 9/10/11)
4. **Self-consistency of locking system itself** (H2 12/13/14/15) ←
   tier 4 born from L65 silently 漂的事件

### 13.5 Honesty corrections (L72, L75)

- **L72**: OK(84) cppunit total 是 51 provider + 33 cui = 8 idx + 8
  fuzzy + 10 recent + **7 controller**。Workdir 仅 verify 77 (前 4
  binaries)；7-case `cui_commandpalette_controller` 在 SRCDIR
  (`cui/qa/unit/CommandPaletteControllerTest.cxx`) 但 BUILDDIR
  workdir 无 `.test.log` → OK(84) 是 **claimed**, 不是 verified。
- **L75**: 尝试 `make CppunitTest_cui_commandpalette_controller`
  升级 77→84 失败 — harfbuzz meson `UnicodeDecodeError byte 0xe5
  position 13` 因 BUILDDIR 根含非 ASCII `可点office`。这是 **B2-class**
  build-env 阻塞，不是 wall-clock。Log: `/tmp/cppunit-controller-build.log`
  (1561 行)。所以 OK(84) upgrade-path = "rename BUILDDIR ASCII-only OR
  patch meson `LC_ALL=C`"，不是 "wait for budget"。

### 14.3 H2 check 16 (新 tier-4 lock, post-L83)

L82 余波审计发现：jq + 朴素 shell string-compare 在 ledger row 5 误报
NON-MONOTONIC，因为 row 1-4 用 `+0800`、row 5-82 用 `+0000`，原始字符串
比较把 `+0800 > +0000`。实际 UTC instants 全 82 行非递减（python
datetime 验证）。check 16 enforce 三件事:

1. ts 必须正则匹配 `[+-][0-9]{4}$`（**禁** 裸 `Z` 后缀和无 tz 格式）
2. ts 必须能被 BSD `date -j -f "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S%z"` 解析为 epoch
3. epoch 必须 ≥ 前一行 epoch（UTC-normalized 非递减）

两个 negative canary 现场跑过：(a) 把最后一行 ts 改成 `2020-01-01...`
触发 backward-UTC FAIL；(b) 改成 `Z` 后缀触发 missing-numeric-tz FAIL。
canary 协议块加进 CLAUDE-NOTES §"Verifying check 12/13/14/15/16
actually catch drift"。

### 14.4 4-tier locking architecture (post-L83)

| Tier | 检查 | 范围 | 自动伸展 |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 schema↔C++ | H1+H4/5/7 | apply-plan/runtime/async-task/inline-action 状态字 | C++ header 落地后 partial→full 自动促进 |
| 2 schema↔manual | H6 | 4 reader's manuals fact-block ↔ schema body | glob-discovered，新 `*.schema.md` 自动入册 |
| 3 lane-status↔artifacts | H2 9/10/11 | ledger-count, manual roster, harness path+0755 | 双向；任一漂移 fail CI |
| **4 self-consistency** | **H2 12/13/14/15/16** | row-shape, baseline 3-site, sweep exec-bit, sweep↔disk parity, **ledger ts ISO+UTC monotonicity** | 锁住 locking 体系自身；L65-L83 一系列事件迭代而成 |

tier-4 在本日累计添加 5 个 self-consistency lock，全部源于 L65 起的
具体 drift 事件：L65 row 多键 → L66 check 12 / L67 baseline 镜像漂移
→ L67 check 13 / L70 sweep 失 0755 → L70 check 14 / L76 新 harness
未入 sweep → L76 check 15 / **L82 ledger ts mixed-tz 字符串比较误报 →
L83 check 16**。每个事件都有具体复现路径 + 现场 negative canary。

### 16.3 H2 check 17 (新 tier-4 lock, post-L89)

3 个 sentinel L-anchor 抽取 + invariant `max - min ≤ 3`:

- (a) `docs/v2-coordinator-handoff-2026-05-10.md` 标题 `(L<N>)`
- (b) `docs/CLAUDE-NOTES.md` `refreshed YYYY-MM-DD / L<N>`
- (c) `docs/product/v2/STATUS-2026-05-11.md` 最新 section header
  `L<X>→L<Y>` max Y across all such ranges

Tolerance 3 的实证依据：

- 紧 (≤ 1 或 ≤ 2)：cadence pattern L74/L78/L82/L85 显示 handoff 自然
  refresh interval 是 4 commits — 强制每 commit touch 3 docs 不现实
- 松 (≥ 5)：让一个完整 append cycle 流过才 catch，等同 L81/L86 的
  手工 cleanup 模式 — 不解决问题
- = 3：当 anchor 漂移到自然 cadence 边缘时 fail，时机正好

Canary 现场跑过 + restore:

- 17A: 把 CLAUDE-NOTES anchor 改 `L85→L77`，gap=11 FAIL with diagnostic
- 17B: 把 handoff title 改 `(L88)→(L82)`，gap=4 FAIL with diagnostic

### 17.3 Canary 8/8 全 verified（L93 turn 现场）

每个 canary：mutate → run harness → FAIL with exit=1 → restore → PASS →
post-restore working-tree clean。本 turn 第一次系统化跑全 8 条，不是
"应该会 fail"声称、是 actually verified.

| canary | check | mutation | mutated result | restore result |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 13 | H2 13 baseline mirror | CLAUDE-NOTES 46→45 | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |
| 14 | H2 14 sweep 0755 | chmod 644 sweep.sh | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |
| 15A | H2 15 sweep↔disk parity | add stub tests/v2-fake-test.sh | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |
| 15B | H2 15 (reverse) | comment harness entry in sweep | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |
| 16A | H2 16 ts ISO+UTC monotonic | bad ts string in ledger | FAIL exit=1 | PASS (after fix) |
| 16B | H2 16 (reverse) | reorder ledger rows | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |
| 17A | H2 17 L-anchor cadence | CLAUDE-NOTES L→L69 | FAIL exit=1 | PASS (after fix) |
| 17B | H2 17 (reverse) | handoff title (L90)→(L80) | FAIL exit=1 | PASS |

8/8 真 catch + 8/8 restore 干净 + 0 leak。Production gate: canary
protocol 从"protocol-level claim"升级为"row-by-row verified"。

### 17.4 暴露并修的 2 个 protocol bug

**16A**：BSD `sed -i.tmp` 留 `.agent/goals/.../ledger.jsonl.tmp` orphan，
未 cleanup → 下次 git status 噪声、潜在 `git add .` 风险。
Fix: `sed -i ''`（empty backup ext，BSD 安全 in-place），并删掉无用的
`rm -f *.tmp` cleanup 行（既然 no .tmp 产生）。

**17A**：原 mutation regex `'refreshed 2026-05-11 / L8[0-9]'` hardcode
日期，CLAUDE-NOTES 实际 anchor 行已是 `refreshed 2026-05-12`，sed 静默
no-op，跑下来 mutated 也 PASS — 假 verified。Fix: date-agnostic regex
`'/ L8[0-9])'` 只锚 L-anchor 段，跨日期稳定。

两个 bug 都是 protocol-doc 落地后从未被 actually-run 暴露 → tier-4
production gate "claimed fail-loud" 与 "verified fail-loud" 的 gap。

## 18. 凌晨增量 IV (2026-05-12 dawn-late III, L94)

> §17 声明"canary 8/8 全 verified"已闭合 protocol drift class，但本节
> 是 §17 自我修正：L93 turn 修了 17A 的 `hardcoded date` 但 **未** 修
> regex 段 `L8[0-9]` — 一旦 anchor 进 L9x（即下一 commit）该 sed 就
> silent no-op，"verified" 实属侥幸。L94 把 17A/17B 双 canary regex
> 改 anchor-agnostic（`L[0-9]+`），并现场跑 mutate→FAIL→restore→PASS
> 实证；这才是 §17 dirft 3-layer closure 的真正完成态。

### 18.1 一句话

L93 自评 "structurally closed" 高估；L94 才真闭合 — 把 canary regex
本身的 anchor-依赖去掉，让 protocol 跨任意 L 段都能 catch drift。

### 18.2 单 commit (L94)

| L# | commit | 内容 |
|---|---|---|
| L94 | 本次 | docs/CLAUDE-NOTES.md canary 17A/17B regex anchor-agnostic 化（`L8[0-9]` → `L[0-9]+` / `L[0-9][0-9]` → `L[0-9]+`），加 inline 注释解释 leak class |

### 18.3 现场 mutate→restore 实证（L94 turn）

| canary | 修后 mutate | 现场 FAIL exit | gap diagnostic | restore exit | leak |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 17A | `sed -E 's|/ L[0-9]+\)|/ L70)|'` 替换 anchor 行 | 1 | gap=23 (max=93 min=70) | 0 | 无 |
| 17B | `sed -E '1s/\(L[0-9]+\)/(L80)/'` 替换 handoff 标题 | 1 | gap=13 (max=93 min=80) | 0 | 无 |

`ls /tmp/*.bak` 后无残留，`bash tests/v2-plan-baseline-test.sh` 47 checks 全绿。

### 18.4 为什么 L93 没发现

L93 turn 跑 17A 时 anchor 仍是 L93 → 旧 regex `L8[0-9]` 不匹配 L93 →
`sed` 静默 no-op → file 未变 → harness PASS → 误判 "exit=1 catch drift"。
**实则没 mutate 成功**。当时也没拿 grep 验文件实际内容。

L94 修后 regex 从 `L8[0-9]` → `L[0-9]+` 让 mutate 在任何 L 数下都生效。
跑 17A: file 真被改成 `L70`, gap=23, harness 真 FAIL — 才是实证 catch。

### 18.5 元教训

"verified-by-run" 不仅是 "跑了 mutate→PASS→FAIL→restore" 步骤；还要
**确认 mutate 真改动了文件内容**。否则 sed regex 失配的 silent no-op
会冒充 "PASS→FAIL→PASS" 的假实证。

加固 protocol：跑完 mutate 后 grep / cat 确认 sentinel 已变（17A 跑完
应看到 `/ L70)`, 17B 应看到 `(L80)`），再跑 harness 才算实证。

### 18.6 L94 后基线

H2 baseline 47 不变（本 turn 改 docs，不改 source）。Sweep 7/7 全绿
（H1=26 H2=47 H3=26 H4 partial H5 partial H6=39 H7 partial）。

3-site mirror & sentinel：CLAUDE-NOTES line 9 anchor `/ L94)`,
handoff title `(L94)`, lane-status `94 entries`, STATUS §18 max-Y=L94 —
gap=0。

### 18.7 仍开放

与 §17.7 完全一致。本 turn 未触 user-only 授权门 + 环境阻塞 + W5
schema↔fixtures gap。

## 19. 凌晨增量 V (2026-05-12 dawn-late IV, L94→L95)

> §17.7/§18.7 列 W5 async-task schema↔fixtures gap "仍开放"。L95 把这条
> gap 闭合：`async-task.schema.json` `state` 枚举 7 值（pending/running/
> review-ready/applied/canceled/failed/expired），但 fixtures 此前只锁
> 了 review-ready（valid）+ canceled（cancelled），剩余 5 态全裸 — 任何
> 非 review-ready/canceled 的 lifecycle 字段 invariant 漂了 schema 都不
> 会 fail-loud。

### 19.1 一句话

补 pending / running / applied 三个 valid fixture，把 W5 lifecycle
state-enum 的 validity 锁从 2/7 提升到 5/7，覆盖 typical happy path
全程；failed / expired 仍开放（低频末端态，下一 wave 再补）。

### 19.2 单 commit (L95)

| L# | commit | 内容 |
|---|---|---|
| L95 | 本次 | NEW docs/schemas/fixtures/async-task.{pending,running,applied}.json + docs/schemas/async-task.schema.md §7 fixture matrix 3→7 行 + tests/v2-plan-baseline-test.sh fixture count 36→39 三处 |

### 19.3 三 fixture 设计

| state | task_id | kind | 关键 invariant 锁 |
|---|---|---|---|
| pending | tk-20260512-001 | outline-to-slides | `result_plan_id: null`, `evidence_ids: []`, 所有 step.state=pending |
| running | tk-20260512-002 | weekly-report | `result_plan_id: null`, 1 step completed (有 evidence), 1 running, 1 pending |
| applied | tk-20260511-005 | contract-review | `result_plan_id: ^ap-[0-9a-f]{16}$`, 全 step completed, `review_decisions: [accept/refine/reject]` |

`state ↔ result_plan_id` 互斥不变量 (pending/running 必须 `null`,
applied 必须匹配 `^ap-[0-9a-f]{16}$`) 现在被 3 valid fixture 显式锁住。

fallback (`bin/intelligent-contract-fixtures.sh` 165-187) 让
`async-task.<state>.json` 自动 expected=valid。

### 23.3 接口锁

```cpp
// sw/inc/docsh.hxx
namespace sw::intelligent {
    struct ApplyPlan;
    struct ApplyResult;
}
class SwDocShell : public SfxObjectShell {
public:
    sw::intelligent::ApplyResult
    applyDiagnosticsPlan(const sw::intelligent::ApplyPlan& rPlan);
};

// sw/source/uibase/app/docst.cxx
sw::intelligent::ApplyResult
SwDocShell::applyDiagnosticsPlan(const sw::intelligent::ApplyPlan& rPlan)
{
    return sw::intelligent::ApplyEngine(*this).run(rPlan);
}
```

`docsh.hxx` **不** include 引擎头（避免 ODR 膨胀；前置声明已足）。

## 25. 下午 / 午夜增量 II (2026-05-13, L102→L102 — survey triangle 完成)

### 25.1 上下文

L101 之后约定的 next-action：在 wrapper 下做 W3.A / W4.A / W2.A 三连 survey，所有都 reversible，不动 SRCDIR。本节记录这三个 survey 的全部结论。Survey artifact 全部在 `tmp/`：

- `tmp/w3-apply-link-survey.log` — 31 行
- `tmp/w4-link-survey.log` — 116 行
- `tmp/w2-cppunit-survey.log` — 45 行

### 25.2 W3.A — `CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine` 不存在于 build system

```
make PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8 CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine
→ gmake[1]: *** No rule to make target 'CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine'.  Stop.
```

SRCDIR 实地核对：

| 期望 | 实际 |
|---|---|
| `sw/CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine.mk` | **缺失** |
| `sw/Module_sw.mk` 注册 apply_engine | **没有** |
| `sw/CppunitTest_*apply*.mk` 任意命名 | 0 个 |
| 已存在的相邻 cppunit | `sw/CppunitTest_sw_inline_actions.mk` |

含义：W3 14-case cppunit "claimed" 状态名义上 H7 full-enforce 已锁 schema 层；但 C++ 这一侧只有源文件没有 build 入口。要让 roadmap §1.1 的"`make CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine` exit 0"达成，**D1 授权除了 `UndoApplyPatch.hxx` + `SwDocShell::applyDiagnosticsPlan` wiring 之外，还要追加一个 build-system sub-step**：新建 `sw/CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine.mk` + 在 `sw/Module_sw.mk` 加一行 `CppunitTest_sw_apply_engine` 注册 + 实际 `sw/qa/.../ApplyEngineTest.cxx` 里 14 case。这是这次 survey 才浮出来的 sub-gap，不是新工作量，但要在 D1 授权前明确范围。

### 25.3 W4.A — 三 surface 错误分类（与 B2 无关，是 source/link 层）

| Surface | 阶段 | 根因 | 修复 scope |
|---|---|---|---|
| sw_inline_actions | **CXX 编译** | `IntelligentWriterAnalyzer.hxx:60` `unknown type name 'SwDocShell'`；`IntelligentWriterApplyEngine.cxx:11` `'UndoApplyPatch.hxx' file not found` | 与 W3.B/W3.C 共享，gated **D1** |
| sc_inline_actions | **链接** | `Undefined symbols: sc::inline_actions::toToken(CellAction)`、`fromToken(OUString const&)`。源 `CellActions.{hxx,cxx}` PRESENT；`Library_sc.mk:370-371` REGISTERED；`CellActions.cxx:14/27` 已实现；问题在 header decl 没 `SC_DLLPUBLIC`，macOS arm64 默认 hidden visibility 把符号在 `libsc.dylib` 边界剔除 | 1 个 header，2 行宏，gated **W4 source/link** |
| sd_inline_actions | **链接** | 同 sc 形态：`sd::inline_actions::{toToken,fromToken}` undefined；`SlideElementActions.{hxx,cxx}` PRESENT、`Library_sd.mk:155-156` REGISTERED、`.cxx:14/26` 已实现、header decl 缺 `SD_DLLPUBLIC` | 1 个 header，2 行宏，gated **W4 source/link** |

按"修复成本最小"排序：sd ＜ sc ≪ sw。sc/sd 各只是 1 个 header 加 `S{C,D}_DLLPUBLIC` 修饰；sw 是 D1 范围里完整 undo-patch family 加 analyzer header 修复。

授权后期望状态：

```
make PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8 CppunitTest_sd_inline_actions  → [build CUT] exit 0
make PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8 CppunitTest_sc_inline_actions  → [build CUT] exit 0
make PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8 CppunitTest_sw_inline_actions  → 还要 D1
```

CppunitTest_cui_commandpalette_fuzzy       → [build CUT] exit 0  → workdir log: OK (8)

- L72 起一直记 "OK(84) claimed / OK(77) workdir-verified"。**今天 OK(77) → OK(84)，对齐**。
- L75 起一直记 "controller 默认环境 fail at harfbuzz Meson"。今天证明 wrapper 应用到 W2 cppunit family 与应用到 W5 cowork（L101）形态完全一致。

### 25.8 风险与陷阱（继承）

- 不要在没 wrapper 的环境下尝试用 `make CppunitTest_*` 触发 harfbuzz Meson；默认环境会重复触发 `UnicodeDecodeError byte 0xe5`（原 B2 现象）。每个本地命令都要带 `PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8`。
- W2 OK(84) workdir-verified 这一资产是 _wrapper-conditional_：换走 `/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8` 这个文件之后会丢。Wrapper 不进 git。如果有人删 `/tmp` 或换机器，需要重建 wrapper。
- W4 sc/sd 的 link 修复看似最小（2 行宏），但触动 SRCDIR header；仍需 W4 source/link 显式授权才能动。

### 26.4 L104b — W1 spec "Cloud Adapter Token Lock" backlog（168 行）

`w1-provider-runtime-spec.md` 追加 §"Cloud Adapter Token Lock (W1.cloud, design-only)"，10 子节：

1. 第一阶段目标 — Anthropic-shape first；OpenAI/Azure/Bedrock 是 V2.x
2. Cloud adapter 接口 — `kqoffice::ai::CloudAdapter` + `Vendor enum` + `Config struct` 7 字段
3. Key storage — 3 OS keychain reference（macOS Security.framework / Windows wincred / Linux libsecret），**绝不存 raw key 到 registry**
4. ServiceMode 切换 evidence — mode-switch-to-cloud reason
5. 请求 lifecycle 增量 — 24h 隐私 ack + cloud-marker
6. Timeouts / 重试 — 4xx 不 retry / 5xx retry 1×1s / 429 立返
7. Anthropic response 字段映射 — `content[0].text` / `usage.input_tokens` / `usage.output_tokens` / `stop_reason`
8. 不在本 backlog — HTTP client 选型 / 多 vendor / streaming / tool use / 计费
9. Gate — W1 cloud (D1d cloud)，落地顺序 W1.A/W1.B 先 → 再 D1d cloud
10. Schema 冻结要点 — Config 7 字段 / vendor=Anthropic / 3 reference scheme / 3 新 evidence 字段

新 evidence 字段（`request_tokens` / `response_tokens` / `stop_reason`）= schema 改动 = H1 + H6 联动；本 backlog **只锁形态，不动 JSON schema，不动 C++ EvidenceRecord**，必须等 D1d cloud 放行后同 PR 一起落，避免 schema 先于 C++。

## 37. W5 Review 打开处理器增量 XIV (2026-06-09, L133→L134 — stored-task review-open handler)

## 60. Visible Cmd+Shift+K CommandPalette Increment XXXVII (2026-06-09, L158→L159)

L159 closes the visible current-bundle Writer CommandPalette shortcut proof. The blocker was not native event injection itself: independent probes showed keyboard input reached the Writer document, and Cmd+K still opened HyperlinkDialog. The root cause was a Writer-family module accelerator override in `officecfg/registry/data/org/openoffice/Office/Accelerators.xcu`: Global `K_SHIFT_MOD1` already mapped to `.uno:CommandPalette`, but `com.sun.star.text.GlobalDocument`, `com.sun.star.text.WebDocument`, and `com.sun.star.text.TextDocument` overrode `K_SHIFT_MOD1` en-US to `.uno:SmallCaps`.

The fix changes those Writer-family `K_SHIFT_MOD1` en-US values to `.uno:CommandPalette`, preserving Cmd+K as `.uno:HyperlinkDialog` and preserving non-Writer module shortcuts. After `gmake officecfg.build postprocess.build`, both `workdir/XcdTarget/main.xcd` and `instdir/可圈office.app/Contents/Resources/registry/main.xcd` carry the new mapping. `bin/v2-visible-current-bundle-smoke.sh` now sends Cmd+Shift+K through native CGEvent on the exact builddir pid and verifies CommandPalette/search/results AX nodes on the same pid before the separate UNO dispatch proof.

Current local result: `Status: passed`, `Target attribution: ready`, 9 passed / 0 blocked / 0 failed. This proves current-bundle V2 entry parity, direct builddir launch, exact AX target binding/drive, GUI Text Document creation, physical Cmd+Shift+K CommandPalette proof, visible `.uno:CommandPalette` dispatch, and CommandPalette AX nodes. It still does not prove Select-to-act visible click-through, DiffReview visible accept/reject, Cowork menu/new task/accept task loops, or the full GUI/worker E2E.

### 60.2 Landing Evidence

| Area | Proof |
|---|---|
| Root cause | Writer-family `K_SHIFT_MOD1` en-US module overrides resolved Cmd+Shift+K to `.uno:SmallCaps` instead of Global `.uno:CommandPalette` |
| Accelerator fix | `officecfg/registry/data/org/openoffice/Office/Accelerators.xcu` maps Writer-family `K_SHIFT_MOD1` en-US to `.uno:CommandPalette` while Cmd+K remains `.uno:HyperlinkDialog` |
| Registry rebuild | `gmake officecfg.build postprocess.build` refreshed generated registry artifacts into the builddir bundle |
| Physical shortcut proof | `bin/v2-visible-current-bundle-smoke.sh` posts Cmd+Shift+K via native CGEvent to the exact builddir pid and sees CommandPalette/search/results AX nodes |
| Current classification | `tmp/v2-visible-current-bundle-smoke.md` reports `Status: passed`, `Target attribution: ready`, 9 passed / 0 blocked / 0 failed |

## 64. Visible Writer Select-to-Act Increment XLI (2026-06-09, L162→L163)

L163 closes the Writer Select-to-act visible click-through gap for the current builddir bundle. The visible smoke initially proved the current pid, Writer document seed, and real text selection, but no popover appeared. The root cause was product-side: the Select-to-act controller was only called from `SwWrtShell::DrawSelChanged()`, while ordinary Writer text selection commits flow through Writer selection/view notification paths.

The source fix wires the controller into normal Writer text selection updates. `sw/source/uibase/uiview/view.cxx` now calls `sw::inline_actions::OnWriterSelectionChanged(*m_pWrtShell)` after `SelectShell()` in `AttrChangedNotify` and after delayed `NotifySelChanged()` in `TimeoutHdl`. `sw/source/uibase/wrtsh/select.cxx` also calls the controller after `EndSelect()` finishes UI selection logging. The controller still owns the eligibility checks, including non-empty single-paragraph text selection and the `LO_RUNNING_UI_TEST` skip guard.

`bin/v2-visible-select-to-act-smoke.sh` is a new strict current-bundle visible smoke. It launches the builddir app with an isolated Writer profile and UNO socket, seeds a paragraph through bundled pyuno, focuses the visible Writer window, creates a real text selection with native AX/CGEvent, verifies the selected text through UNO, scans the exact pid AX tree for `SelectToActPopover`, `btn_rewrite`, `btn_expand`, and `btn_shorten`, clicks `Rewrite paragraph`, and treats popover closure after the click as dispatch evidence. The script exits nonzero only for real failures; blocked states remain reportable without failing the shell.

### 64.2 Landing Evidence

| Area | Proof |
|---|---|
| Product hook | normal Writer text selection updates now call `OnWriterSelectionChanged` from `view.cxx` and `select.cxx` |
| Visible smoke | `bin/v2-visible-select-to-act-smoke.sh` |
| Text selection proof | bundled pyuno reports `selection_state=ok count=1 text_len=38` |
| AX popover proof | exact builddir pid exposes `SelectToActPopover`, `btn_rewrite`, `btn_expand`, and `btn_shorten` |
| Click-through proof | `Rewrite paragraph` receives `AXPress` and the Select-to-act popover closes after the click |

## 67. Visible Cowork Pending/Running Rows Increment XLIV (2026-06-10, L165→L166)

L166 adds stable current-bundle UI proof for Cowork `pending` and `running` rows while retaining the real L165 review/apply loop. `bin/v2-visible-cowork-smoke.sh` seeds one envelope for each state in its isolated current-month TaskStore, opens the real Cowork dialog on the exact builddir pid, and requires AX-visible `[pending]` and `[running]` rows. It then removes only those seeded envelopes before pressing New Task, preventing the fixture pending task from being scheduled ahead of the real click-through task.

The first extended run intentionally surfaced that interference boundary: the seeded pending row was picked by TaskQueue and left the newly clicked task pending. After cleanup was moved between the visibility assertions and the real New Task click, the full smoke passed again. This proves the product UI renders both states, but does not claim that the current synchronous New Task handler visibly transitions through them in real time.

## 68. Nonblocking Cowork Transition Increment XLV (2026-06-10, L166→L167)

L167 replaces the Cowork New Task synchronous UI path with a real nonblocking bridge. `CoworkUiTaskBridgeJob::prepare()` writes the new task as `pending` immediately, `CoworkDialog` refreshes that selected row, and a VCL `AutoTimer` starts the worker from the dialog's main-thread poll loop. The worker then exposes a real `running` interval before completing to `awaiting-review`; completion is polled back on the main thread, preserving the selected task and enabling the existing accept path.

The DiffReview handoff remains safe: the background job reports through the same review-open sink, and `ShowDiffReviewPanel` already marshals worker callbacks to the VCL main thread with `Application::PostUserEvent`. `CoworkDialog` stops the poll timer and joins the job before cleanup, so the review sink is not destroyed while the worker still owns a reference.

## 70. Visible DiffReview Real Ollama Provider Increment XLVII (2026-06-10, L168→L169)

## 75. UITest Start Center Writer Creation Increment LII (2026-06-10, L173→L174)

L174 resolves the remaining W4 UITest svp root cause instead of routing around it. The hang was in `vcl/source/uitest/uno/uiobject_uno.cxx`: after `executeAction("CLICK")` invoked the Start Center Writer button, `ExecuteWrapper::ExecuteActionHdl` waited for a `TaskPriority::LOWEST` idle to signal completion. Writer frame creation can keep lower-priority idles postponed while events continue to reschedule, so the Python UITest caller never got control back even though the button handler had already dispatched `private:factory/swriter`.

The fix changes only that post-action completion idle to `TaskPriority::DEFAULT`. `sw/qa/uitest/selectToAct/test_select_to_act.py` now adds `test_writer_start_center_create_smoke`, which creates Writer through `self.ui_test.create_doc_in_start_center("writer")`, asserts `com.sun.star.text.TextDocument`, and verifies the resulting top focus window exposes `writer_edit`.

### 75.2 Verification

| Command | Result |
|---|---|
| `MAKE=gmake gmake vcl.build PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8` | passed |
| `python3 -m py_compile /Users/lu/kdoffice-src/sw/qa/uitest/selectToAct/test_select_to_act.py` | passed |
| `rm -rf workdir/UITest/demo_ui && MAKE=gmake gmake UITest_demo_ui UITEST_TEST_NAME='command_with_parameters.CommandWithParametersTest.test_text_color_change' PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8` | passed; `done.log` reports `Ran 1 test`, `OK`, with `OnNew` observed through the Start Center route |
| `rm -rf workdir/UITest/sw_select_to_act && MAKE=gmake gmake UITest_sw_select_to_act PKG_CONFIG=/tmp/kqoffice-pkgconf-utf8` | passed; `done.log` reports `Ran 4 tests`, `OK`, `Tests run: 4`, `failed=0`, `errors=0`, `skipped=0` |

`docs/schemas/knowledge-index-result.schema.json` locks the result envelope: queryId linkage, workspace parity, resultCount and latency bounds, retrievalMode parity, ranked chunk references, `scoreBasisPoints`, `textHash`, `snippetHash`, sha256 boundary, `storesDocumentContent=false`, no public egress, and evidence ids shaped like `ev-[0-9a-f]{16}`. Paired fixtures under `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/knowledge-index-query-result/` cover keyword document FTS, hybrid connector private retrieval, semantic local hybrid retrieval, plus invalid guards for raw query text, raw result snippet/document content, public-egress cloud drift, and result/topK/latency drift.

`tests/v3-knowledge-index-query-result-test.sh` validates both schemas, the 3 valid / 3 invalid paired fixture roster, query/result linkage, workspace parity, `topK` / resultCount / latency invariants, source-kind coverage, hash-only snippets, no raw content fields, no public egress, and cross-links from W3/W5/master plan docs, `bin/v3-eval-sweep.sh`, and `.github/workflows/v3-contract-harnesses.yml`. ## 90. V3 Companion Contract Self-Test Increment LXVII (2026-06-10, L188→L189)

`docs/schemas/companion-pairing-token.schema.json` locks the pairing envelope: id, schemaVersion, createdAt/expiresAt, tenant/workspace, desktop instance, proposed device, transport, token, security, data boundary, and evidence. The contract fixes 10-minute pairing token TTL, 24h device session intent, hash-only token storage, device binding, PIN confirmation, mTLS, revocation, LAN gRPC default on port 17801, and no document-content storage.

`docs/schemas/companion-diff-summary.schema.json` locks the mobile read-only diff summary envelope: task and step-result refs, Writer/Calc/Impress surface, ApplyPlan runtime ref without mobile ApplyPlan parsing, V2 action-kind parity (`ParagraphAction`, `CellAction`, `SlideElementAction`), changed-object hash refs, redacted/hash-only storage, view-only mobile cache, no mobile editing, no offline approval, and required evidence links.

`docs/schemas/companion-approval-request.schema.json` locks the online approval envelope: task/summary/pairing refs, user actor, `channel=companion`, awaiting-review/failure-recovery states, approve/reject/rollback actions, LAN push default via W8 port 17801, enterprise push only with `cloudPushOptIn`, `biometricRequired=true`, second confirmation, `mobileMayEdit=false`, audit log required, and no offline approval.

Fixtures under `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/companion/` cover LAN/enterprise pairing, Writer/Calc/Impress diff summaries, LAN/enterprise approval requests, plus invalid guards for long-lived pairing tokens, diff summaries storing document content, offline approval, and public push without opt-in. `tests/v3-companion-contract-test.sh` validates all three schemas, the 7 valid / 4 invalid fixture roster, semantic invariants, raw-content guard markers, and cross-links from W7/W5/master plan docs, `bin/v3-eval-sweep.sh`, and `.github/workflows/v3-contract-harnesses.yml`. It is deliberately not H13; H8-H12 remain the V3 numbered contract harnesses.

`docs/schemas/i18n-locale-policy.schema.json` locks the locale policy: supported launch locales zh-CN/en-US/ja-JP/zh-TW, UI locale follows OS locale through existing i18npool, silent locale switching forbidden, AI output default locale matches UI locale, explicit-only `/lang` override, no silent persistence, required evidence markers, embedded/online manual baseline zh-CN/en-US, GA blocking, V2 regression requirement, and `runtimeImplementation=not-started`.

## 101. V3 In-App Chat Entry-Route Design Increment LXXVIII (2026-06-10, L199→L200)

L200 tightens the V3 W1 in-app-chat entry-route contract while keeping accelerator registration, CommandPalette runtime fallback implementation, sidebar runtime registration, provider/apply wiring, and product integration gated. The key correction is that W1 does not claim a second direct `Cmd+Shift+K` binding: `Cmd+Shift+K` remains the V2 CommandPalette entry path, and W1 Chat is reached through `command-palette-chat-fallback` into the `sfx2-sidebar` surface.

`docs/product/v3/w1-keyboard-shortcut-survey.md` locks the accepted route, the `directAcceleratorRegistration=false` guard, and the no-`officecfg`-registration rule before explicit implementation authorization. `docs/product/v3/w1-sidebar-uiwireframe.md` locks the design-only sidebar surface, required states, and non-goals: no standalone chat app, no new W1 schema, no direct accelerator registration, no WebView requirement, and no stored prompt/raw document content in fixtures.

All W1 in-app-chat fixtures now declare `route=command-palette-chat-fallback` and `directAcceleratorRegistration=false`; `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/in-app-chat/invalid/direct-accelerator-registration.json` rejects the direct-binding drift. `tests/v3-in-app-chat-test.sh` now validates the shortcut survey, sidebar wireframe, 4 valid fixtures, 5 invalid guards, CommandPalette fallback route, V2 Provider/ApplyPlan/evidence reuse, no W1 schema, and runtime-not-started gates.

## 102. V3 In-App Chat Context Syntax Increment LXXIX (2026-06-10, L200→L201)

L201 activates the V3 W1 explicit context syntax contract while keeping parser, autocomplete, context extraction, connector runtime fetch, sidebar UI behavior, provider/apply wiring, and product integration gated. The contract prevents W1 Chat from silently capturing document content: valid context must be explicit and limited to `@selection`, `@doc`, or `@connector:<id>`.

`docs/product/v3/w1-context-syntax-policy.md` locks the mention grammar, requires `defaultScope=none` plus non-empty `explicitMentions`, forbids implicit full-document context, rejects unknown mentions, keeps connector context read-only with `data-fetch` evidence, and forbids raw document/prompt/selection/connector content in fixtures. This remains a design contract only; it authorizes no parser or runtime implementation.

`docs/qa/fixtures/v3/in-app-chat/valid/writer-doc-summary.json` adds explicit `@doc` coverage. The new invalid guards `implicit-full-doc-context.json`, `unknown-context-mention.json`, and `connector-write-context.json` reject silent full-document capture, unsupported mention syntax, and connector write-back drift. `tests/v3-in-app-chat-test.sh` now validates 5 valid fixtures, 8 invalid fixtures, the context syntax policy document, CommandPalette fallback route, V2 Provider/ApplyPlan/evidence reuse, no W1 schema, and runtime-not-started gates.

## 104. V3 In-App Chat History Locality Increment LXXXI (2026-06-10, L202→L203)

L203 activates the V3 W1 per-document local chat history contract while keeping SQLite storage, document-id derivation, sidebar persistence, clear-history UI behavior, migration code, provider/apply wiring, and product integration gated. `docs/product/v3/w1-chat-history-policy.md` locks `history.scope=per-doc-local`, `history.storage=local-sqlite-sidecar`, `history.documentBinding=document-id-hash`, `history.cloudSync=false`, `history.globalIndex=false`, `history.crossDocumentRestore=false`, `history.rawContentInFixture=false`, `history.requiresUserClearControl=true`, and `history.deleteWithDocument=true`. This remains a design/fixture contract only; it authorizes no storage, migration, sidebar persistence, or document-binding implementation.

All W1 in-app-chat fixtures now declare a `history` envelope. The new invalid guards `global-history-leakage.json`, `cloud-history-sync.json`, `raw-transcript-history.json`, and `missing-history-clear-control.json` reject global leakage, cloud sync, raw transcript fixture storage, and missing user clear/delete behavior. `tests/v3-in-app-chat-test.sh` now validates 5 valid fixtures, 15 invalid fixtures, the history policy document, explicit context syntax, Markdown subset rendering, CommandPalette fallback route, V2 Provider/ApplyPlan/evidence reuse, no W1 schema, and runtime-not-started gates.

## 106. V3 In-App Chat Context Autocomplete Increment LXXXIII (2026-06-10, L204->L205)

L205 activates the V3 W1 context autocomplete/no-conflict contract while keeping mention popup rendering, parser/autocomplete runtime, connector suggestion runtime, sidebar UI behavior, provider/apply wiring, and product integration gated. This remains a design/fixture contract only; it authorizes no parser, popup, connector suggestion runtime, or Office autocomplete hook implementation.

All W1 in-app-chat fixtures now declare a `mentionsUi` envelope. The new invalid guards `global-autocomplete-hijack.json`, `unknown-connector-suggestion.json`, `raw-context-preview.json`, and `autocomplete-runtime-parser-started.json` reject global Office autocomplete interception, unknown connector suggestions, raw context preview/storage, and early parser/autocomplete runtime claims. `tests/v3-in-app-chat-test.sh` now validates 5 valid fixtures, 23 invalid fixtures, the context autocomplete policy document, explicit context syntax, Markdown subset rendering, per-doc local history, streaming UI states, CommandPalette fallback route, V2 Provider/ApplyPlan/evidence reuse, no W1 schema, and runtime-not-started gates.

## 107. V3 Connector Manifest Trust Chain Increment LXXXIV (2026-06-10, L205->L206)

L206 activates the V3 W2 connector manifest trust-chain contract while keeping manifest installer UI, signature verification runtime, connector registry runtime, `Connectors.xcu` registration, marketplace submission, OAuth/API key flow code, and product integration gated. The contract resolves W2 Q4 by making manifest source, publisher identity, digest pinning, review state, install scope, and unsigned-manifest rejection explicit and H8-verifiable.

`docs/product/v3/w2-manifest-trust-policy.md` locks the trust envelope fields `source`, `publisher`, `manifestSha256`, `reviewState`, `installScope`, `signatureRequired`, and `allowUnsigned`. `docs/schemas/connector-manifest.schema.json` now requires `trust` at the top level, forbids extra trust properties, restricts trust sources to `builtin`, `community`, and `enterprise-admin`, requires `sha256:` plus 64 lowercase hex chars, and keeps `allowUnsigned=false`.

All seven built-in connector fixtures now declare built-in trust with `publisher=kqoffice`, `reviewState=repo-reviewed`, `installScope=builtin`, `signatureRequired=true`, `allowUnsigned=false`, and pinned manifest hashes. The invalid connector roster now includes `missing-manifest-hash.json`, `tenant-scope-without-approval.json`, `unsigned-community-manifest.json`, and `unreviewed-community-manifest.json`, alongside the existing evidence, offline-mode, and cloud-confidential guards. `tests/v3-connector-manifest-contract-test.sh` now validates 7 valid fixtures, 7 invalid fixtures, trust schema shape, built-in trust semantics, community security-review semantics, tenant-approved semantics, signature requirement, and unsigned rejection while keeping H8 at 16 checks.

## 114. V3 Eval Report Archive Policy Lock Increment XCI (2026-06-10, L212→L213)

## 118. V3 Agent Step Resume Policy Lock Increment XCV (2026-06-10, L216→L217)

L217 activates the V3 W6 cross-session resume policy lock while keeping AgentRuntime, Planner, Actor, Observer, ShadowDoc serialization, resume runtime, checkpoint persistence, scheduler parallelism, source integration, and product runtime implementation gated. The contract resolves W6 Q5 by deciding that long tasks may resume after app restart only from evidence-complete checkpoints.

`docs/product/v3/w6-resume-policy.md` now locks `crossSessionResumeAllowed=true`, `resumePoint=evidence-complete-checkpoint`, `requiresUserConfirmation=true`, `requiresDocumentHashMatch=true`, `requiresShadowSnapshot=true`, `requiresAuditReplay=true`, `autoResumeAllowed=false`, `staleCheckpointBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, `checkpointEvidence=required`, and `runtimeResumeImplementation=not-started`.

`docs/schemas/agent-step-plan.schema.json` now requires `resumePolicy` metadata. All W6 plan fixtures carry the resume-policy envelope, and `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/agent-step-plan/invalid/stale-checkpoint-auto-resume.json` rejects stale checkpoint / auto-resume drift. `tests/v3-agent-step-plan-test.sh` now validates the policy document, schema consts, resume semantics, invalid stale checkpoint guard, dependency/validation/approval policy mirrors, W6/master/W5/sweep mirrors, and reports `Checks: 11`.

## 121. V3 Knowledge Index Model Acquisition Policy Lock Increment XCVIII (2026-06-11, L219→L220)

L220 activates the V3 W3 Knowledge Index model acquisition policy lock while keeping model downloader runtime, embedding runtime, vector index runtime, public egress, source integration, and product runtime implementation gated. The contract resolves W3 Q1 by deciding that BGE-m3 must not be hidden in the installer or fetched by background network activity.

`docs/product/v3/w3-model-acquisition-policy.md` now locks BGE-m3 as not bundled by default and never silently downloaded. Hybrid/vector retrieval requires explicit user confirmation before model download, offline/missing/declined model states fall back to SQLite FTS5, public egress is false by default, and both `runtimeDownloaderImplementation` and `runtimeEmbeddingImplementation` remain `not-started`.

`docs/schemas/knowledge-index-chunk.schema.json` now requires `modelAcquisitionPolicy` metadata. All valid W3 chunk fixtures carry the policy envelope, and `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/knowledge-index-chunk/invalid/model-acquisition-silent-download.json` rejects bundled or silent BGE-m3 download drift, public egress by default, and runtime downloader/embedding start before the W3 gate. `tests/v3-knowledge-index-chunk-test.sh` now validates the policy document, schema consts, fixture semantics, invalid silent-download guard, W3/master/W5/sweep mirrors, and reports `Checks: 8`.

## 123. V3 Knowledge Index Watcher Scalability Policy Lock Increment C (2026-06-11, L221→L222)

L222 activates the V3 W3 Knowledge Index watcher scalability policy lock while keeping watcher runtime, OS-specific file watcher integration, index scheduling runtime, source integration, and product runtime implementation gated. The contract resolves W3 Q3 by forbidding one file descriptor per indexed file and defining the large-workspace fallback behavior before runtime watcher code exists.

`docs/product/v3/w3-watcher-scalability-policy.md` now locks `trigger=background-watcher`, `debounceMs=5000`, `largeWorkspaceThresholdFiles=10000`, `largeWorkspaceStrategy=bounded-watch-plus-polling-fallback`, `perFileDescriptorWatch=false`, `maxOpenFileDescriptors=256`, `pollingFallbackIntervalSeconds=60`, `overflowBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeWatcherImplementation=not-started`.

`docs/schemas/knowledge-index-chunk.schema.json` now requires `watcherPolicy` metadata. All valid W3 chunk fixtures carry the policy envelope, and `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/knowledge-index-chunk/invalid/watcher-per-file-fd-runtime.json` rejects per-file descriptor watch drift, missing debounce/fallback, excessive fd budget, silent overflow drops, and runtime watcher implementation before the W3 gate. `tests/v3-knowledge-index-chunk-test.sh` now validates the watcher policy document, schema consts, fixture semantics, invalid watcher guard, W3/master/W5/sweep mirrors, and reports `Checks: 10`.

## 124. V3 Knowledge Index Extraction Policy Lock Increment CI (2026-06-11, L222→L223)

L223 activates the V3 W3 Knowledge Index extraction policy lock while keeping extraction runtime, standalone parsers, source integration, and product runtime implementation gated. The contract resolves W3 Q4 by deciding that PPT/PPTX text extraction must follow the LibreOffice import filter and the Impress document model rather than a separate parser path.

`docs/product/v3/w3-extraction-policy.md` now locks document extraction to `textExtractionPath=document-model` for Writer/Calc/Impress documents, requires `usesLibreOfficeImportFilter=true` and `usesDocumentModel=true`, maps PPTX to `documentFamily=impress` / `inputFormat=pptx`, requires `preservesSlideElementRefs=true` for PPTX chunks, forbids `standalonePptParserAllowed`, and keeps `runtimeExtractionImplementation=not-started`.

`docs/schemas/knowledge-index-chunk.schema.json` now requires `extractionPolicy` metadata. Valid W3 chunk fixtures now include `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/knowledge-index-chunk/valid/impress-pptx-slide-fts.json`, and `docs/qa/fixtures/v3/knowledge-index-chunk/invalid/ppt-standalone-parser-runtime.json` rejects standalone PPT parser drift, bypassed LibreOffice import filters, missing Impress document-model use, lost slide element refs, and runtime extraction start before the W3 gate. `tests/v3-knowledge-index-chunk-test.sh` now validates the extraction policy document, schema consts/enums, fixture semantics, invalid standalone-parser guard, W3/master/W5/sweep mirrors, and reports `Checks: 11`.

## 125. V3 Knowledge Index Storage Policy Lock Increment CII (2026-06-11, L223→L224)

## 129. V3 W1 Content Review Policy Lock Increment CVI (2026-06-11, L227→L228)

L228 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around content review. Content review is no longer just a boolean support flag: W1 now requires a visible evidence-linked content diff review surface for selection, document-section, connector-result, Knowledge Index result, evidence record, and task-step suggestions.

`docs/product/v3/w1-content-review-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.contentReview.scope`, `reviewMode=evidence-linked-content-diff`, `visible=true`, `usesDiffReview=true`, `requiresEvidenceLink=true`, `requiresHumanApproval=true`, `mainDocumentUnchangedUntilApproval=true`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `suggestionContentInFixture=false`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeContentReviewImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `content-review-missing-envelope.json`, `content-review-no-evidence.json`, `content-review-mutable-suggestion.json`, and `content-review-runtime-started.json` reject missing review metadata, review without DiffReview/evidence, direct-rewrite mutation before approval, raw/suggestion fixture content, and premature runtime claims.

## 130. V3 W1 Artifact Navigator Policy Lock Increment CVII (2026-06-11, L228→L229)

## 131. V3 W1 Review Queue Policy Lock Increment CVIII (2026-06-11, L229→L230)

L230 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around review management. Content review and formatting review items must not only appear as individual chat replies or one-off DiffReview panels: W1 now requires a visible queue for content-review, formatting-review, and task-step review items.

`docs/product/v3/w1-review-queue-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.reviewQueue.visible=true`, `itemTypes=[content-review,formatting-review,task-step]`, `states=[queued,open,approved,rejected,applied,failed]`, `filterBy=[state,type,surface]`, `openUsesDiffReview=true`, `requiresEvidenceLink=true`, `bulkActions=[approve-selected,reject-selected]`, `bulkApplyRequiresExplicitHumanApproval=true`, `mainDocumentMutationAllowed=false`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeReviewQueueImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `review-queue-missing-envelope.json`, `review-queue-no-filter.json`, `review-queue-bulk-auto-apply.json`, and `review-queue-runtime-started.json` reject missing queue metadata, missing filters/states, batch auto-apply or DiffReview bypass, main-document mutation before approval, raw review fixture content, and premature runtime claims.

## 133. V3 W1 Interaction Chrome Policy Lock Increment CX (2026-06-11, L231→L232)

L232 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around interaction and style. The W1 AI surface must not collapse back into a chat modal: it needs a compact native sidebar workbench that keeps chat, tasks, artifacts, reviews, and evidence inspection reachable as first-class panels.

`docs/product/v3/w1-interaction-chrome-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.interactionChrome.layout=sidebar-workbench`, `navigation=segmented-tabs`, `panels=[chat,tasks,artifacts,reviews,evidence]`, `defaultPanel=chat`, `persistentComposer=true`, `taskRailVisible=true`, `artifactRailVisible=true`, `reviewRailVisible=true`, `evidenceRailVisible=true`, `keyboardNavigation.tabOrder=[composer,panel-tabs,active-panel,review-actions]`, `keyboardNavigation.escapeReturnsFocus=true`, `keyboardNavigation.focusTrap=false`, `density=compact-utility`, `usesNativeControls=true`, `modalChatOnly=false`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeInteractionChromeImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `interaction-chrome-missing-envelope.json`, `interaction-chrome-modal-only.json`, `interaction-chrome-no-keyboard.json`, and `interaction-chrome-runtime-started.json` reject missing chrome metadata, modal-only chat, hidden rails, mouse-only/focus-trapped navigation, raw fixture content, non-native controls, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.

## 136. V3 W1 Workspace Filter/Search Policy Lock Increment CXIII (2026-06-11, L234→L235)

L235 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around finding and narrowing AI work products. W1 now requires visible metadata-only filter/search across tasks, artifacts, reviews, evidence, and previews, so content review, formatting review, evidence inspection, and artifact management are navigable without indexing raw document or prompt content.

`docs/product/v3/w1-workspace-filter-search-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.filterSearch.visible=true`, `scope=[current-workspace,current-document]`, `surfaces=[tasks,artifacts,reviews,evidence,previews]`, `filterBy=[state,type,surface,source,evidence-status]`, `searchFields=[id,type,state,source-metadata,evidence-id,hash-reference]`, `sortOptions=[recent-first,type,state,source]`, `metadataOnly=true`, `hashOnlyReferences=true`, `redactsRawPayload=true`, `rawContentIndexed=false`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `crossDocumentSearch=false`, `globalIndex=false`, `usesContentOpeners=true`, `requiresEvidenceLink=true`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeFilterSearchImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `filter-search-missing-envelope.json`, `filter-search-scope-drift.json`, `filter-search-raw-index.json`, and `filter-search-runtime-started.json` reject missing filter/search metadata, scope/surface/filter/search-field drift, raw content indexing, non-hash references, opener/evidence bypass, global or cross-document indexing, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.

## 137. V3 W1 Workspace Context Handoff Policy Lock Increment CXIV (2026-06-11, L235→L236)

L236 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around opening and carrying context across surfaces. W1 now requires visible handoff state when users move from search results, artifact items, review queue items, evidence links, preview items, or action-bar commands into preview, DiffReview, evidence inspection, review queues, task progress, or the composer.

`docs/product/v3/w1-workspace-context-handoff-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.contextHandoff.visible=true`, `entrySurfaces=[filter-search-result,artifact-navigator-item,review-queue-item,evidence-inspector-link,preview-matrix-item,action-bar-command]`, `handoffTargets=[preview,diff-review,evidence-inspector,review-queue,task-progress,composer]`, `preserves=[active-task-id,source-surface,evidence-id,hash-reference,preview-mode,review-state]`, `requiresVisibleBreadcrumb=true`, `requiresBackNavigation=true`, `requiresFocusReturn=true`, `requiresEvidenceLink=true`, `usesContentOpeners=true`, `usesDiffReview=true`, `metadataOnly=true`, `hashOnlyReferences=true`, `redactsRawPayload=true`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `previewContentInFixture=false`, `mainDocumentMutationAllowed=false`, `autoApplyAllowed=false`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeContextHandoffImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `context-handoff-missing-envelope.json`, `context-handoff-target-drift.json`, `context-handoff-raw-payload.json`, and `context-handoff-runtime-started.json` reject missing handoff metadata, target/preserve drift, missing breadcrumb/back/focus return, opener/DiffReview/evidence bypass, raw payload handoff, auto-apply, main-document mutation, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.

## 138. V3 W1 Workspace Review State Sync Policy Lock Increment CXV (2026-06-11, L236→L237)

L237 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around synchronized review state. W1 now requires review queue, DiffReview, preview matrix, evidence inspector, task progress, and action bar surfaces to expose the same queued/open/approved/rejected/applied/failed state and the same open/approve/reject/apply/fail transition semantics.

`docs/product/v3/w1-workspace-review-state-sync-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.reviewStateSync.visible=true`, `stateSources=[review-queue,diff-review,preview-matrix,evidence-inspector,task-progress,action-bar]`, `states=[queued,open,approved,rejected,applied,failed]`, `syncTargets=[review-queue,diff-review,preview-matrix,evidence-inspector,task-progress,action-bar]`, `transitionEvents=[open,approve,reject,apply,fail]`, `requiresEvidenceLink=true`, `requiresVisibleState=true`, `requiresHumanApproval=true`, `bulkApplyRequiresExplicitHumanApproval=true`, `usesDiffReview=true`, `usesContentOpeners=true`, `metadataOnly=true`, `hashOnlyReferences=true`, `redactsRawPayload=true`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `mainDocumentMutationAllowed=false`, `autoApplyAllowed=false`, `conflictBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeReviewStateSyncImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `review-state-sync-missing-envelope.json`, `review-state-sync-target-drift.json`, `review-state-sync-auto-apply.json`, and `review-state-sync-runtime-started.json` reject missing review-state metadata, source/target/state/transition drift, missing evidence or visible state, DiffReview/content opener bypass, raw review-state payloads, auto-apply, main-document mutation, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.

W1 now requires chat, tasks, artifacts, reviews, evidence, previews, and action bar surfaces to expose a chronological append-only activity trail for AI requests, task starts, artifact creation, opened content, review openings, review-state changes, evidence links, invoked actions, and visible failures.

## 142. V3 W1 Workspace Native Style Policy Lock Increment CXIX (2026-06-11, L240→L241)

L241 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around native workbench style and density. W1 now requires AI-assisted review, formatting, opening, evidence, preview, and task surfaces to stay in a compact native sidebar workbench instead of drifting into a card pile, modal-only chat, or marketing-style hero layout.

`docs/product/v3/w1-workspace-native-style-policy.md` locks `workspaceUi.nativeStyle.layout=sidebar-workbench`, `density=compact-utility`, `surfaces=[composer,panel-tabs,task-rail,artifact-rail,review-queue,evidence-inspector,preview-matrix,action-bar]`, `navigation=segmented-tabs`, `usesNativeControls=true`, `stableDimensions=[toolbar-buttons,tab-badges,task-rows,review-rows,evidence-rows,preview-tiles]`, `textOverflowPolicy=wrap-or-ellipsize-no-overlap`, `cardPileLayout=false`, `modalOnly=false`, `marketingHero=false`, `keyboardAccessible=true`, `focusReturn=true`, `metadataOnly=true`, `rawContentInFixture=false`, `previewContentInFixture=false`, `transcriptContentInFixture=false`, `mainDocumentMutationAllowed=false`, `autoApplyAllowed=false`, `failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible`, and `runtimeNativeStyleImplementation=not-started`. The new invalid guards `native-style-missing-envelope.json`, `native-style-density-drift.json`, `native-style-card-layout.json`, and `native-style-runtime-started.json` reject missing native style metadata, density/surface/navigation/stable-dimension drift, text-overlap policy drift, card-pile/modal-only/marketing layouts, missing keyboard/focus return, raw style payloads, auto-apply, main-document mutation, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.

## 143. V3 W1 Workspace Content Registry Policy Lock Increment CXX (2026-06-11, L241→L242)

L242 refines the Codex-style AI workspace direction around content object management and opening. W1 now requires documents, selections, connector results, Knowledge Index results, evidence records, task steps, review items, formatting previews, and content suggestions to be registered as metadata-only workspace objects before they can be opened, previewed, reviewed, inspected, or resumed.

docs/product/v3/w1-workspace-content-registry-policy.md locks workspaceUi.contentRegistry visible=true, scope=[current-workspace,current-document], types=[document,selection,connector-result,knowledge-index-result,evidence-record,task-step,review-item,formatting-preview,content-suggestion], states=[registered,opened,previewed,in-review,applied,failed,archived], requiredFields=[object-id,type,source-surface,state,evidence-id,hash-reference,open-target,preview-mode], openTargets=[main-document-window,sidebar-preview,diff-review,evidence-inspector,review-queue], previewModes=[metadata-summary,read-only-preview,diff-preview,evidence-summary], usesContentOpeners=true, usesPreviewMatrix=true, usesEvidenceInspector=true, usesReviewQueue=true, metadataOnly=true, hashOnlyReferences=true, redactsRawPayload=true, rawContentInFixture=false, previewContentInFixture=false, transcriptContentInFixture=false, mainDocumentMutationAllowed=false, autoOpenAllowed=false, autoApplyAllowed=false, failureBehavior=fail-closed-user-visible, and runtimeContentRegistryImplementation=not-started. The new invalid guards content-registry-missing-envelope.json, content-registry-type-drift.json, content-registry-raw-payload.json, and content-registry-runtime-started.json reject missing registry metadata, type/state/field/target drift, raw payload exposure, automatic opening/apply, main-document mutation, silent failure, and premature runtime claims.
